### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="1654" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1658" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="1666" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="1678" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="1692" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="1699" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphism closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2380" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

<!-- We say that a class 𝒦 is **closed under** `H` (or `H`-**closed**) provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

--------------------------------

#### <a id="subalgebra-closure">Subalgebra closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras that are closed under the taking of subalgebras as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3145" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3161" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3166" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3168" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3169" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3171" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3173" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3175" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3183" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3185" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3187" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3189" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3194" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3195" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3203" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3205" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3206" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3208" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3209" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3213" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3216" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3219" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3224" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3225" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3233" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3236" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3239" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3241" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3242" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3244" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3245" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a><a id="3247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3248" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3250" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3252" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3253" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3256" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="S.sbase"></a><a id="3264" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3264" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="3270" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3272" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3273" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3273" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3275" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3277" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3287" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3288" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3290" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3292" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3273" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3294" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3296" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3298" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3300" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="3309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3273" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3311" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3313" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3317" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `S` (or `S`-**closed**) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` -->

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras closed under arbitrary products is the following. 

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3948" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3953" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3955" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3956" <a id="3976" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3982" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3990" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3993" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="3995" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3998" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3999" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4002" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4004" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4010" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4018" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4019" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4021" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4023" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3958" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4024" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4026" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883"   <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4340" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4343" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4397" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3972" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4400" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4402" class="Symbol">→</a> <a   <a id="P.pisou"></a><a id="4416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4416" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a>  <a id="4423" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4425" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4426" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4482" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4443" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4484" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4486" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4443" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4488" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4490" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4492"   <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4496" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4496" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4503" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4505" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4506" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4508" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4512" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4520" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4522" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4523" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4525" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4527" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4529" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4531" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4533" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4534" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4536" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3958" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4537" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4539" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3972" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4541" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4543" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4545" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4547" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4549" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4551" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4553" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4555" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4557" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3972" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="variety-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will typically denote it by `V`.

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="5223" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="5228" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5230" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5231" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5233" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5235" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5237" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5245" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5247" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5249" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5251" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5257" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5265" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5267" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5268" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5270" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5273" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5274" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5277" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="5280" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5285" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5286" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5294" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5295" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5297" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5300" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5302" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5303" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5305" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a><a id="5307" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5308" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5310" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5312" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5313" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5316" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5324" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5333" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5334" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5338" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5346" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5348" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5349" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5351" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5353" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5355" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5357" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5359" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5361" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5370" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5372" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5374" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5378" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties since we will need them later.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6317" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s expansive.</a>
<a id="P-expa"></a><a id="6376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6376" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="6383" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6385" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6386" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6386" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6388" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6390" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6398" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6400" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6400" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6404" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6410" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6386" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6420" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6421" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6423" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6426" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6386" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6427" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6430" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6432" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6400" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6434" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6436" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6437" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6438" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6386" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6439" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6441" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6386" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6442" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6444" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6400" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="6446" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6376" class="Function">P-expa</a><a id="6452" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6453" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6453" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6454" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6456" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6456" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="6457" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6459" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6460" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6460" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6461" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6463" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="6466" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6468" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4416" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="6473" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6474" class="Argument">𝑨</a> <a id="6476" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6478" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6479" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6488" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6460" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6490" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6453" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6491" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="6494" class="Argument">𝑩</a> <a id="6496" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6498" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6460" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6499" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6501" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6502" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4048" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="6508" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Bound">KA</a><a id="6510" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6512" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6513" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="6519" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="6529" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6532" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s idempotent.</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="7751" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7751" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="7764" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7766" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7767" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7767" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7769" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7769" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="7771" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7773" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="7781" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7783" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7783" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7785" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7787" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="7792" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7793" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="7801" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7767" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7803" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="7804" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7806" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="7809" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7767" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7810" class="Symbol">)}</a>
               <a id="7828" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7829" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7829" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="7831" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7833" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="7841" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7842" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7767" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7844" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="7846" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7769" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7847" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7849" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="7850" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7852" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7854" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7829" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="7856" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2049" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="7876" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7783" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
               <a id="7893" class="Comment">---------------------------------------------------</a>

  <a id="9512" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="9521" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9521" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9524" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9526" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9495" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9528" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2049" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="9548" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8242" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

   <a id="9622" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9622" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="9627" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9495" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9631" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="9633" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9635" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9577" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="9638" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="12562" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12562" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12567" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12569" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12252" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12572" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="12574" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12192" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="12578" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12562" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12583" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12585" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3811" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="12593" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12252" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12596" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12192" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12598" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12599" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="12605" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="12615" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12617" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12207" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the short term objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13707" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13709" class="Argument">𝓘</a> <a id="13711" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13713" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13062" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="13714" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13716" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13068" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13720" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13068"     <a id="13762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13762" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="13766" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13768" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Basic.html#2093" class="Function">is-homomorphism</a> <a id="13784" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13785" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13787" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13170" class="Function">SA</a><a id="13789" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13791" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13792" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13794" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13125" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="13795" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13797" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13596" class="Function">i</a>
    <a id="13803" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13762" class="Function">iii</a> <a id="13807" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13809" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="13811" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13811" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="13813" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13813" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="13815" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13817" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1902" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="13821" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="13823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13825" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13828" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="13832" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13834" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13407" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="13839" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13841" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="13842" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13844" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13811" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="13846" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13849" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13849" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13851" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13853" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13813" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="13855" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13849" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13857" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">i</a><a id="13858" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13863" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13863" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="13865" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13867" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13869" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13125" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="13871" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="13873" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="13875" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13065" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="13879" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13863" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="13881" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13883" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4250" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a><a id="13888" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13889" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13059" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13890" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13892" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13062" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="13893" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13895" class="Argument">I</a> <a id="13897" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13073" class="Bound">I</a><a id="13900" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13902" class="Argument">𝒜</a> <a id="13904" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13906" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13125" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="13907" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13909" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13912" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13912" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13914" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13916" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6376" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="13923" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13924" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13225" class="Function">KA</a> <a id="13927" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13912" class="Bound">i</a><a id="13928" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="13934" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13934" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="13936" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13938" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13940" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13076" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="13942" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="13944" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13946" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13170" class="Function">SA</a>
  <a id="13951" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13934" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="13953" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13955" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="13958" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1902" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="13962" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13278" class="Function">B≅SA</a>

</pre>

#### PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="14156" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14163" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14163" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14165" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14166" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14166" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14168" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14170" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="14178" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14180" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14180" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14182" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14184" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="14189" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14190" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14198" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14166" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14200" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14201" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14203" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14206" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14166" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14207" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14210" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14211" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14211" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14215" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14217" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14225" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14226" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14229" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14166" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14230" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14232" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14235" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14166" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14236" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14239" class="Keyword">where</a>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play in our formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem.

<a id="16417" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16191" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16421" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16422" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="16428" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16428" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16429" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16431" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16433" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5826" class="InductiveConstructor">vprodw</a> <a id="16440" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="16443" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16443" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="16445" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16447" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16191" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16451" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16452" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16428" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16454" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16443" class="Bound">i</a><a id="16455" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="16458" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16191" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16462" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16463" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4416" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="16469" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16469" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16471" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16471" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="16473" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16475" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16477" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5908" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a> <a id="16483" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16484" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16191" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16488" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16469" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16489" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16491" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16471" class="Bound">x₁</a>
<a id="16494" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16191" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16498" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16499" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4496" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="16505" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16505" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16507" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16507" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="16509" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16511" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16513" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5988" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="16519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16520" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16191" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16524" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16505" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16525" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16527" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16507" class="Bound">x₁</a>

<a id="SP⊆V"></a><a id="16531" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16536" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16538" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16539" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16539" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16541" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16541" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="16543" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16545" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="16553" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16555" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16555" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16559" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16565" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16573" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16539" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16575" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16576" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16578" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16581" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16539" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16582" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="16586" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="16591" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="16592" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16593" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16539" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16595" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="16597" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16541" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16598" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16600" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16539" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16602" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="16604" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16541" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16605" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16607" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16608" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16609" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16539" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16611" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16613" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16541" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16614" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16616" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16555" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16619" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="16621" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="16622" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16623" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16539" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16624" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16626" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16541" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16627" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16555" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="16631" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16636" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16637" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3264" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="16642" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16643" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16643" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16644" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16646" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16646" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="16651" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16653" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16655" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16191" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="16659" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16660" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4496" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="16666" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16646" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="16672" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="16682" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="16684" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16690" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3321" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="16695" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16696" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16696" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16697" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16699" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16699" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16700" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16702" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16704" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5448" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="16711" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16712" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16717" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16699" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16718" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="16720" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a><a id="16724" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16725" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16725" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16726" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16728" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16728" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16729" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16731" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16732" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16733" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16735" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16736" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3386" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="16740" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16741" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16741" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16742" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16744" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16744" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16745" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16747" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16747" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="16751" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16751" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="16754" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16756" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16758" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5679" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="16765" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16766" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16771" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16747" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="16774" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16776" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16751" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="16780" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a><a id="16784" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16785" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16785" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16786" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16788" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16788" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="16789" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16791" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16792" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16792" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16793" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16796" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3465" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="16801" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16802" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16802" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16803" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16805" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16805" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16806" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16808" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16808" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="16812" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16812" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="16815" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16817" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16819" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5679" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="16826" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16808" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="16835" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16837" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16812" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="16841" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16846" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16847" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3529" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16852" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16852" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16854" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16854" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="16856" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16858" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16860" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5988" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="16866" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16867" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16531" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="16872" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16852" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16873" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16875" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16854" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="products-of-classes">Products of classes</a>

Next we formally state and prove that, given an arbitrary class 𝒦 of algebras, the product of all algebras in the class S(𝒦) belongs to SP(𝒦). That is, ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦 ). This turns out to be a nontrivial exercise. In fact, it is not immediately obvious (at least not to this author) how one expresses the product of an entire class of algebras as a dependent type. Nonetheless, after a number of failed attempts, the right type revealed itself. (Not surprisingly, now that we have it, it seems almost obvious.)

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="17475" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product"></a><a id="17482" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17482" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="17496" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17497" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17497" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17499" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17501" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17509" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17511" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17511" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17513" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17515" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17520" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17521" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17529" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17497" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17531" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17532" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17534" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17537" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17497" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17538" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17541" class="Keyword">where</a>

</pre>

First, we define the type that will serve to index the class (as well as the product of its members), as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.ℑ"></a><a id="17690" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17690" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="17692" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17694" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17695" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17695" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17697" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17699" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17707" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17709" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="17712" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17717" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17718" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17726" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17695" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17728" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17729" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17731" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17734" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17695" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17735" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17737" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17740" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17743" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17695" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17744" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17746" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="17749" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17690" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="17751" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17752" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17752" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17753" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17755" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17755" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17757" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17759" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="17761" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17761" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="17763" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="17765" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17766" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17774" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17752" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17776" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17777" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17779" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="17781" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17761" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="17783" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="17785" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17755" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Taking the product over this index type ℑ requires a function like the following, which takes an index (i : ℑ) and returns the corresponding algebra.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.𝔄"></a><a id="17966" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17966" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="17968" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17970" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17971" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17971" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17973" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17975" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17983" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17985" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17985" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17987" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17989" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17994" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17995" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18003" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17971" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18005" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18006" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18008" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18011" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17971" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18012" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18015" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18017" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17690" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18019" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17985" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18021" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18023" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18031" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17971" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18033" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18036" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17966" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18037" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18038" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18038" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18039" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18041" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18041" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18042" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18044" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18046" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18049" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18049" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18051" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18053" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18054" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17690" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18056" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18041" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18057" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18060" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18062" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18064" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18049" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18066" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Finally, the product of all members of 𝒦 is represented as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.class-product"></a><a id="18165" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18165" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18179" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18181" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18182" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18182" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18184" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18186" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18194" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18196" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18198" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18204" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18182" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18215" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18217" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18220" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18182" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18221" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18223" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18225" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18233" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18234" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18237" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18182" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18238" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18240" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18243" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18165" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18257" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18258" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18259" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18261" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18261" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18263" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18265" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18267" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18269" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17966" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18270" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18271" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18258" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18272" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18274" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18261" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18275" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18277" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Alternatively, we could have defined the class product in a way that explicitly displays the index, like so.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="18417" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18417" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="18432" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18434" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18435" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18435" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18439" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18447" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18449" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18451" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18456" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18457" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18465" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18435" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18467" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18468" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18470" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18473" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18435" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18474" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18476" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18478" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18486" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18487" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18490" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18435" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18491" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18493" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18496" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18417" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a><a id="18510" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18511" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18511" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18512" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18514" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18514" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18516" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18518" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18520" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18523" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18523" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18525" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18527" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18528" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18530" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18530" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18532" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18534" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18535" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18543" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18511" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18546" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18548" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18550" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18530" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18552" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18554" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18514" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18555" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18558" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18560" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18562" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18523" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18564" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

If `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, then we can think of the pair `(𝑨 , p) ∈ ℑ 𝒦` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p)` (which is obviously `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} )` onto the `(𝑨 , p)`-th component.


#### ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
Finally, we prove the result that plays a leading role in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem---namely, that our newly defined class product ⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} ) belongs to SP(𝒦).

As we just saw, the (informal) product ⨅ S(𝒦) of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as ⨅ ( 𝔄 {𝓤}{S(𝒦)} ), and our goal is to prove that this product belongs to SP(𝒦). We can do this by first proving that the product belongs to PS(𝒦) (in `class-prod-s-∈-ps`) and then applying the PS⊆SP lemma above.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19365" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product-inclusions"></a><a id="19372" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19372" class="Module">class-product-inclusions</a> <a id="19397" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19398" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19398" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19400" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19402" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19410" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19412" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19413" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19413" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19415" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19417" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19423" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19431" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19398" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19433" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19434" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19436" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19439" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19398" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19440" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19443" class="Keyword">where</a>
 <a id="19450" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="19455" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17482" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="19469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19470" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19472" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19474" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19398" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19475" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19477" class="Argument">𝒦</a> <a id="19479" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19481" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19413" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19482" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.𝓸𝓿𝓾"></a><a id="19485" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19485" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a> <a id="19489" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19491" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a>

   <a id="19672" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19672" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19675" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19675" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19679" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19681" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17690" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19683" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19684" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19685" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19686" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19398" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19687" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19689" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19398" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19690" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19692" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19413" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19693" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19695" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19697" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19705" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19706" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19485" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19709" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19711" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a>

   <a id="19879" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19844" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="19885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19885" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19887" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19889" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4048" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a><a id="19894" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19895" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19897" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19899" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19900" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19485" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19903" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="19906" class="Argument">𝓦</a> <a id="19908" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19910" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19911" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19485" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19914" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19917" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19918" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19782" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="19922" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19885" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19923" class="Symbol">)</a>

   <a id="19929" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19929" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19936" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19938" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="19940" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19675" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19944" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19946" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="19948" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19949" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19951" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19413" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19952" class="Symbol">)</a>

   <a id="20004" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20004" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="20010" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20012" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20014" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20014" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20016" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20018" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20019" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19675" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="20023" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20014" class="Bound">i</a><a id="20024" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20026" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="20028" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20029" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17966" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="20031" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20014" class="Bound">i</a><a id="20032" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="20037" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20004" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="20043" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20043" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20045" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20047" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3811" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="20055" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20056" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19675" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="20060" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20043" class="Bound">i</a><a id="20061" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20063" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20064" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17966" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="20066" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20043" class="Bound">i</a><a id="20067" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20069" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20070" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="20076" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="20086" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20088" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20089" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="20095" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="20105" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="20109" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="20209" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20209" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20227" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20229" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a><a id="20236" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20237" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19485" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20240" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20242" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19485" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20245" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20247" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20249" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18165" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="20263" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20264" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="20266" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19413" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20267" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20269" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="20271" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="20272" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20273" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="20275" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19413" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20276" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="20279" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20209" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20297" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20297" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="20301" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20303" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14276" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a><a id="20308" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20309" class="Argument">hfe</a> <a id="20313" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20297" class="Bound">hfe</a><a id="20318" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20320" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19514" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>
